I_PRP was_VBD waiting_VBG for_IN Major_NNP Joslen_NNP 's_POS return_NN to_TO discus9_VB the_DT matter_NN with_IN him_PRP ;_: but_CC as_IN he_PRP unfortunately_RB fell_VBD ill_RB shortly_RB after_IN his_PRP$ return_NN and_CC has_VBZ again_RB taken_VBN leave_VBP I_PRP must_MD wait_VB for_IN Mr._NNP Sowerby_NNP 's_POS return_NN from_IN leave_JJ next_JJ month_NN ,_, and_CC will_MD then_RB discuss_VB the_DT matter_NN with_IN him_PRP and_CC address_NN you_PRP on_IN the_DT subject_NN ._.
4_CD ._.
It_PRP is_VBZ noticeable_JJ that_IN only_RB 47_CD students_NNS at_IN the_DT College_NNP belong_NN to_TO this_DT Presidency_NNP ,_, and_CC that_IN of_IN them_PRP 16_CD are_VBP Government_NNP scholars_NNS ,_, that_WDT is_VBZ to_TO say_VB ,_, only_RB 31_CD paying_VBG students_NNS come_VBP from_IN the_DT Presidency_NNP ._.
The_DT supply_NN of_IN trained_JJ men_NNS is_VBZ ,_, however_RB ,_, equal_JJ to_TO the_DT demand_NN ._.
5_CD ._.
I_PRP have_VBP recently_RB addressed_VBN you_PRP on_IN the_DT subject_NN of_IN the_DT selection_NN of_IN the_DT Government_NNP scholars_NNS and_CC stated_VBD that_IN in_IN my_PRP$ opinion_NN the_DT existing_VBG method_NN of_IN selecting_VBG them_PRP is_VBZ not_RB calculated_VBN to_TO get_VB the_DT class_NN of_IN students_NNS which_WDT we_PRP want_VBP ._.
I_PRP have_VBP suggested_VBN that_IN instead_RB of_IN waiting_VBG for_IN boys_NNS to_TO come_VB to_TO us_PRP ,_, we_PRP should_MD hunt_VB for_IN the_DT right_JJ class_NN in_IN the_DT High_NNP Schools_NNP throughout_IN the_DT Presidency_NNP ._.
The_DT remarks_NNS of_IN the_DT Principal_NNP bear_NN out_IN my_PRP$ previous_JJ contention_NN ;_: and_CC I_PRP trust_VBP that_IN the_DT system_NN will_MD soon_RB be_VB altered_VBN ;_: since_IN the_DT future_NN of_IN the_DT Civil_NNP Veterinary_NNP Department_NNP depends_VBZ on_IN our_PRP$ getting_VBG the_DT right_JJ class_NN of_IN men_NNS ._.
I_PRP have_VBP the_DT honour_NN to_TO be_VB ,_, Sir_NNP ,_, Your_NNP most_RBS obedient_JJ servant_NN ,_, G._NNP E._NNP KEATINGE_NNP ,_, Director_NNP of_IN Agriculture_NNP ._.

134_CD L._NNP OF_IN 1908_CD ._.
From_IN MAJOR_NNP E._NNP JOSLEN_NNP ,_, F.R.C.V.S._NNP ,_, I.C.V.D._NNP ,_, Principal_NNP ,_, Bombay_NNP Veterinary_NNP College_NNP ;_: To_TO THE_DT SECRETARY_NNP TO_NNP GOVERNMENT_NNP ,_, Revenue_NNP Department_NNP ,_, Bombay_NNP ._.

Sir_NNP ,_, I_PRP have_VBP the_DT honour_NN to_TO submit_VB the_DT Annual_NNP Report_NNP of_IN the_DT Glanders_NNP and_CC Farcy_NNP Department_NNP in_IN Bombay_NNP for_IN the_DT year_NN 1907-08_RB ._.
Mr._NNP M._NNP H._NNP Sowerby_NNP ,_, I.C.V.D._NNP ,_, was_VBD in_IN charge_NN of_IN the_DT Department_NNP from_IN the_DT 7th_CD December_NNP 1907_CD to_TO the_DT 6th_CD March_NNP 1908_CD ,_, while_IN I_PRP was_VBD on_IN special_JJ leave_NN ._.
2_CD ._.
During_IN the_DT year_NN under_IN review_NN 142_CD horses_NNS were_VBD admitted_VBN into_IN the_DT Gov-_NNP ernment_NN Lazaretto_NNP at_IN Sewree_NNP as_IN against_IN 197_CD and_CC 33_CD in_IN 1906-1907_JJ and_CC 1905-_JJ 1906_CD ,_, respectively_RB ._.

During_IN this_DT year_NN up_RB to_TO the_DT 8th_CD May_NNP the_DT charge_NN of_IN this_DT Department_NNP was_VBD held_VBN by_IN Major_JJ Joslen_NNP ._.

2_CD ._.
During_IN this_DT year_NN 128_CD horses_NNS were_VBD admitted_VBN into_IN the_DT Government_NNP Lazaretto_NNP at_IN Sewree_NNP as_IN against_IN 142_CD and_CC 197_CD in_IN 1907-08_JJ and_CC 1906-07_JJ ,_, respect-_JJ ively_RB ._.

Out_IN of_IN the_DT 15_CD Contacts_NNS ,_, 4_CD reacted_VBD to_TO the_DT Mallein_NNP test_NN and_CC were_VBD destroyed_VBN ,_, one_CD proved_VBD to_TO be_VB suffering_VBG from_IN Surra_NNP and_CC was_VBD also_RB destroyed_VBN ,_, and_CC 10_CD were_VBD returned_VBN to_TO their_PRP$ owners_NNS as_IN they_PRP were_VBD found_VBN to_TO be_VB free_JJ from_IN disease_NN ._.
The_DT total_JJ number_NN of_IN horses_NNS destroyed_VBN for_IN Glanders_NNP during_IN this_DT year_NN was_VBD 27_CD as_IN against_IN 29_CD and_CC 41_CD in_IN 1907-08_JJ and_CC 1906-07_JJ ,_, respectively_RB ._.
Two_CD horses_NNS suffer-_JJ ing_VBG from_IN Epizootic_JJ Lymphangitis_NNP were_VBD destroyed_VBN as_IN against_IN 1_CD and_CC 2_CD in_IN 1907-08_JJ and_CC 1906-07_JJ ,_, respectively_RB ._.
Seventy-two_JJ horses_NNS suffering_VBG from_IN Surra_NNP were_VBD destroyed_VBN as_IN against_IN 73_CD and_CC 144_CD in_IN 1907-08_JJ and_CC 1906-07_JJ ,_, respectively_RB ._.
Of_IN the_DT 27_CD horses_NNS destroyed_VBN for_IN Glanders_NNP ,_, 17_CD belonged_VBD to_TO Arab_NNP dealers_NNS ,_, 2_CD to_TO Persian_NNP dealers_NNS ,_, 4_CD to_TO private_JJ individuals_NNS ,_, 3_CD to_TO owners_NNS of_IN carriages_NNS plying_VBG for_IN hire_NN ,_, and_CC 1_CD was_VBD ownerless_NN ._.

The_DT different_JJ classes_NNS of_IN horses_NNS admitted_VBN into_IN the_DT Sewree_NNP Lazaretto_NNP this_DT year_NN were_VBD as_IN follows_VBZ :16_VBP The_DT Australian_JJ imports_NNS were_VBD 1,946_CD horses_NNS and_CC 348_CD ponies_NNS as_IN against_IN 2,516_CD horses_NNS and_CC 340_CD ponies_NNS and_CC 2,347_CD horses_NNS and_CC 300_CD ponies_NNS in_IN 1907-08_JJ and_CC 1906-07_JJ ,_, respectively_RB ._.

This_DT year_NN 31_CD American_NNP and_CC 3_CD Arab_NNP donkeys_NNS and_CC 148_CD Persian_JJ and_CC 1_CD Arab_JJ mules_NNS were_VBD imported_VBN ._.
Of_IN the_DT total_JJ above_NN mentioned_VBD imports_NNS 14_CD horses_NNS were_VBD sent_VBN to_TO the_DT Sewree_NNP Lazaretto_NNP from_IN the_DT Harbour_NNP ,_, 9_CD as_IN suspicious_JJ and_CC 5_CD as_IN Contacts_NNS ._.

4_CD ._.
There_EX were_VBD six_CD consignments_NNS of_IN horses_NNS from_IN Queensland_NNP ._.
5_CD ._.
